	-- -------------------------------------------------------------
    -- acl Policy group
    -- -------------------------------------------------------------	
	aclPolicyTable  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX     SEQUENCE OF AclPolicyEntry
        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS     current
        DESCRIPTION
			"A table to configure policy rules in the system."
		::= { aclPolicy 1 }

	aclPolicyEntry OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX     AclPolicyEntry
        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS     current
        DESCRIPTION
              "Each entry in this table is a L3 filter rule.
         Index to the table is L3 filter number. "
        INDEX { aclPolicyIndex }
        ::= { aclPolicyTable 1 }

	AclPolicyEntry ::=
            SEQUENCE {
              aclPolicyIndex                		Integer32,              
              aclPolicySrcMac                   	MacAddress,
			  aclPolicySrcMacMaskLen             	Integer32,
			  aclPolicyDstMac           			MacAddress,
			  aclPolicyDstMacMaskLen    			Integer32,              
              aclPolicyVlanId                   	Integer32,
			  aclPolicy1pPriority             		Integer32,
			  aclPolicyEtherType          			Integer32,
			  aclPolicyTrafficClass      			Integer32,
			  aclPolicyIpType						INTEGER,
              aclPolicySrcIp                   		InetAddress,
			  aclPolicySrcIpMaskLen             	InetAddressPrefixLength,
			  aclPolicyDstIp           				InetAddress,
			  aclPolicyDstIpMaskLen    				InetAddressPrefixLength,              
              aclPolicyDscp                   		Integer32,
			  aclPolicyProtocol             		Integer32,
			  aclPolicySrcPort           			Integer32,
			  aclPolicyDstPort    					Integer32,
			  aclPolicyAction    					INTEGER,
			  aclPolicyReplaceDSCP    				Integer32,
			  aclPolicyReplaceCos    				Integer32,
			  aclPolicySequence    					Integer32,
			  aclPolicyRateLimit    				Unsigned32,
			  aclPolicyPortList    					PortList,
			  aclPolicyEnable						INTEGER,
			  aclPolicyRowStatus   					RowStatus
            }

	aclPolicyIndex OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      Integer32 
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-only 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "Policy rule number."
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 1 }

	aclPolicySrcMac OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        MacAddress
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "Source MAC address."
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 2 } 
		
	aclPolicySrcMacMaskLen OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        Integer32 (0..48)
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "Source MAC mask length.
			1-48: length in bits
			0: Ignored"      
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 3 } 
	
	aclPolicyDstMac OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        MacAddress
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "Destincmon MAC address."
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 4 } 

	aclPolicyDstMacMaskLen OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        Integer32 (0..48)
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "Destincmon MAC mask length.
			1-48: length in bits
			0: Ignored"      
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 5 } 
  
	aclPolicyVlanId OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        Integer32 (0..4093)
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "802.1Q Vlan Id.
			1-4093: Vlan Id
			0: Ignored"	  
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 6 } 
   
	aclPolicy1pPriority OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        Integer32 (-1..7)
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "802.1p priority. 
			0-7: 802.1p priority value      
			-1: Ignored"	  
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 7 } 
   
	aclPolicyEtherType OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX        Integer32 (0..65535)
	   MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	   STATUS    current
	   DESCRIPTION
		  "EtherType. 
			0-65535: EtherType number 
			0: Ignored"	  
	   ::=  { aclPolicyEntry 8 } 
   
    aclPolicyTrafficClass OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      Integer32  (-1..255)
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "IPV6 traffic class for matched packet, it is used in COS.By Default, the value
		  will be '-1', which means the rule don't care this condition."
	  DEFVAL  { -1 }
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 9 } 
	
	aclPolicyIpType OBJECT-TYPE	
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
				ipv4 (1),
				ipv6 (2)
			}
    MAX-ACCESS     read-write
    STATUS         current
    DESCRIPTION
       "The type of IP address used by this classifier entry.  While
       other types of addresses are defined in the InetAddressType

       textual convention, and DNS names, a classifier can only look at
       packets on the wire. Therefore, this object is limited to IPv4
       and IPv6 addresses."
    ::= { aclPolicyEntry 10 }
			
	aclPolicySrcIp OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX         InetAddress
	   MAX-ACCESS     read-create
	   STATUS         current
	   DESCRIPTION
		   "The IP address to match against the packet's source IP address.
		   This may not be a DNS name, but may be an IPv4 or IPv6 prefix.
		   aclClassifierSrcIpMaskLen indicates the number of
		   bits that are relevant."
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 11 }
	
	aclPolicySrcIpMaskLen OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX         InetAddressPrefixLength
		UNITS          "bits"
		MAX-ACCESS     read-create
		STATUS         current
		DESCRIPTION

		   "The length of the CIDR Prefix carried in
		   issAclPolicySrcIpAddr. In IPv4 addresses, a length of 0
		   indicates a match of any address; a length of 32 indicates a
		   match of a single host address, and a length between 0 and 32
		   indicates the use of a CIDR Prefix. IPv6 is similar, except that
		   prefix lengths range from 0..128."
		DEFVAL         { 0 }
		::= { aclPolicyEntry 12 }
	
	aclPolicyDstIp OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX         InetAddress
		MAX-ACCESS     read-create
		STATUS         current
		DESCRIPTION
		   "The IP address to match against the packet's destination IP
		   address. This may not be a DNS name, but may be an IPv4 or IPv6
		   prefix.  aclClassifierDstIpMaskLen indicates the
		   number of bits that are relevant."
		::= { aclPolicyEntry 13 }

	aclPolicyDstIpMaskLen OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX         InetAddressPrefixLength
		UNITS          "bits"
		MAX-ACCESS     read-create
		STATUS         current
		DESCRIPTION
		   "The length of the CIDR Prefix carried in
		   aclPolicyDstIpAddr. In IPv4 addresses, a length of 0
		   indicates a match of any address; a length of 32 indicates a
		   match of a single host address, and a length between 0 and 32
		   indicates the use of a CIDR Prefix. IPv6 is similar, except that
		   prefix lengths range from 0..128."
		DEFVAL         { 0 }
		::= { aclPolicyEntry 14 }
	
	aclPolicyDscp		OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX		Integer32 (-1..63)
		MAX-ACCESS	read-create
		STATUS		current
		DESCRIPTION
			" The IP Dscp value to be checked against the packet. 
			A value of '-1' means, the Dscp Field becomes dont care."
		DEFVAL	{ -1 }
		::= { aclPolicyEntry 15 }
		
	aclPolicyProtocol OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      Integer32 (0..255)
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  " The type of protocol to be checked against the packet. The
		  default value is 0. If the value is 0, it means that the
		  protocol type can be anything and it will not be checked to 
		  decide the action. "
	   DEFVAL   { 0 }
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 16 }
   
	aclPolicySrcPort OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      Integer32 (0..65535)
		MAX-ACCESS  read-write
		STATUS      current
		DESCRIPTION
			"The TCP / UDP source port. The default value is 0, 
			which means the rule don't care this condition."
		DEFVAL   { 0 }
		::= { aclPolicyEntry 17 }
	
	aclPolicyDstPort OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      Integer32 (0..65535)
		MAX-ACCESS  read-write
		STATUS      current
		DESCRIPTION
			"The TCP / UDP destination port. The default value is 0, 
			which means the rule don't care this condition."
		DEFVAL   { 0 }
		::= { aclPolicyEntry 18 }
	
	aclPolicyAction OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      INTEGER {
					  permit (1),
					  deny  (2)
				   }
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "Specifies the action to be taken on the packet if the filter
		  rule matches.
		  If the action is 'Permit', the packet will be forwarded according
		  to the forwarding rules.
		  If the action is 'Deny', the packet will be discarded."
	   DEFVAL  { permit } 
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 19 }
		
	aclPolicyReplaceDSCP	 OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      Integer32 (-1..63)
		MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
		STATUS      current 
		DESCRIPTION 
			"ReplaceDSCP for matched packet.When aclPolicyReplaceDSCP was set to one of 0~63, 
					then aclPolicyReplaceCos will be reset to -1." 
		DEFVAL  { -1 }       

	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 20 }
   
    aclPolicyReplaceCos OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      Integer32  (-1..7)
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "802.1p priority for matched packet. By Default, the value
		  will be '-1', which means the rule don't care this condition.
		  When aclPolicyReplaceCos was set to one of 0~7, 
					then aclPolicyReplaceDSCP will be reset to -1."
	   DEFVAL  { -1 }
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 21 }  
	   
	aclPolicySequence OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..65535)
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "The priority of the filter can be used to decide which filter rule
		   is applicable when 
			  --> the packet matches with more than one filter rules
			  --> All the filter rules result in 'allow'ing the packet

		  Higher value of 'L3 filter priority' implies a higher priority.
		  Usage of 'L3FilterPriority' is implementation dependant."
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 22 }
	   
	aclPolicyRateLimit OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      Unsigned32 (1..65535)
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "Rate limit for matched packet."
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 23 }	
	   
	aclPolicyPortList OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      PortList
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-write 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
		  "Specifies the complete set of ports over which if the packet arrives
		  this filter rule will be applicable.
		  If the incoming port list is '0', the filter rule is applicable for all the 
		  incoming ports.

		  By default inport list is maintained as '0'." 
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 24 }

	aclPolicyEnable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX      INTEGER {
				enabled(1),
				disabled(2)
				}
	MAX-ACCESS    read-write
	STATUS    current
	DESCRIPTION
	  "The object enable/disable acl policy."	  
	::=  { aclPolicyEntry 25 } 
	
	aclPolicyRowStatus OBJECT-TYPE 
	   SYNTAX      RowStatus
	   MAX-ACCESS  read-create 
	   STATUS      current 
	   DESCRIPTION 
			"This object indicates the status of this entry. An entry is
			created in this table when this object is SET to 'createAndWait'.
			The entry in this table is used when the status of this object 
			is SET 'active'. The entry in this table is not used when this 
			object is SET 'notInService'. An entry created in this table is
			be deleted when this object is SET 'destroy'."
	   ::= { aclPolicyEntry 26 }

	-- -------------------------------------------------------------
    -- link aggregation port channel group
    -- -------------------------------------------------------------
	laPortChannelTable  OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX     SEQUENCE OF LaPortChannelEntry
        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS     current
        DESCRIPTION
			"A Port-channel is created through ifMain table.
           	After the creation of the port-channel, corresponding logical
           	interface will be created in the ifMain table. 
           	This Port-channel table is indexed through Key values and allows to 
           	configure link selection policy and the Mac address for 
           	the port-channel. All other objects in this table displays 
           	the details of the port-channel"
		::= { laPortChannel 1 }

	laPortChannelEntry OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX     LaPortChannelEntry
        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS     current
        DESCRIPTION
              "There is one entry in this table for each created port-channel port"
        INDEX { laPortChannelIfIndex }
        ::= { laPortChannelTable 1 }

	LaPortChannelEntry ::=
            SEQUENCE {
              laPortChannelIfIndex                	InterfaceIndex,              
              laPortChannelMode                   	INTEGER,
			  laPortChannelMemberList             	PortList,
			  laPortChannelActivePortList           PortList,
			  laPortChannelStandbyPortList        	PortList
            }

	laPortChannelIfIndex OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
        MAX-ACCESS  read-only
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION
              "The ifIndex of the port-channel(Aggregator's interface index). "
        ::= { laPortChannelEntry 1 }

	laPortChannelMode OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX INTEGER  {
    		 active(1),
    		 passive(2),
			 manual(3),
			 disabled(4)
        }
       	MAX-ACCESS   read-write
       	STATUS       current
       	DESCRIPTION
         	"Current Operating Channel Mode of the port	
				active(1)    - it will always send frames along the configured links.
				passive(2)   - If the actor and partner are both in passive mode, they do not 
								exchange LACP packets.				
				manual(3)  - force the port to enable channeling (Manual).
				disabled(4) - channeling is disabled."
				 
				
		::= { laPortChannelEntry 2 }
		
	laPortChannelMemberList OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX      PortList
        MAX-ACCESS  read-write
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION
              "Member Port list of the port channel. Add the ports as a 
	        aggregation member associated of a port-channel."
        ::= { laPortChannelEntry 3 }
	
	laPortChannelActivePortList OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX      PortList
        MAX-ACCESS  read-only
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION
              "This object will give the member Port list that are attached to the 
				port-channel and actively carrying data traffic on the link."
        ::= { laPortChannelEntry 4 }
	
	laPortChannelStandbyPortList OBJECT-TYPE
	   SYNTAX       PortList
	   MAX-ACCESS   read-only
	   STATUS       current
	   DESCRIPTION
	       "This object will give the port list that are standby due to 
         port-channel have attach port limitation."
	   ::= { laPortChannelEntry 5 }	

    -- -------------------------------------------------------------
    -- link aggregation port control group
    -- -------------------------------------------------------------
	laPortTable OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF LaPortEntry
      	MAX-ACCESS         not-accessible
      	STATUS             current
      	DESCRIPTION
         	"A table that contains objects to set the port lacp mode
         	of laPortTable."
		::={laPort 1 }

	laPortEntry OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      LaPortEntry
		MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
		STATUS      current
		DESCRIPTION
         	"Each entry in this table is for each physical port that participates 
         	in Link Aggregation which can be either aggregatable or individual.
         	This table is indexed by the PortIndex."
		INDEX {laPortIndex }
		::={laPortTable 1 }

	LaPortEntry ::=
		SEQUENCE {
			laPortIndex                         InterfaceIndex,
         	laPortActorPortPriority             INTEGER
        }

	laPortIndex OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX     InterfaceIndex
      	MAX-ACCESS read-only
      	STATUS     current
      	DESCRIPTION
         	"The Index of the port"
      	::={laPortEntry 1 }

	laPortActorPortPriority OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      INTEGER (0..65535)
      	MAX-ACCESS  read-write
      	STATUS      current
      	DESCRIPTION
       		"The priority value assigned to this Aggregation Port.
            This 16-bit value is read-write."
      	::={laPortEntry 2 }
  
	
   dosTable  OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX  SEQUENCE OF DosEntry
        MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
        STATUS  current
        DESCRIPTION
            "A table that holds the DoS settings of the device."
        ::= { sysDos 1 }

    dosEntry OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX  DosEntry
        MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
        STATUS  current
        DESCRIPTION
            "A list of DoS  settings of the device."
        INDEX   { dosType }
        ::= { dosTable 1 }

    DosEntry ::= 
        SEQUENCE {
			dosType           INTEGER,
			dosState          INTEGER
        }
        
    dosType OBJECT-TYPE
    	SYNTAX INTEGER {
			    tcp-syn-pkt-in-data(1),
			    tcp-null-scan(2),
			    tcp_over_mac_mc_bc(3),
			    tcp_fin_urg_psh(4),
			    tcp_syn_rst(5),
			    tcp_udp_port_zero(6),
			    fragmented_icmp(7),
			    arp_sa_mismatch(8)
   	    	}
        MAX-ACCESS  read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
            "This object indicates the DoS  type."
    ::= { dosEntry 1 }
    
	dosState OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX INTEGER {
               deny(1),
               allow(2)
               }
        MAX-ACCESS  read-write
        STATUS  current
        DESCRIPTION
            "This object indicates the status of the DoS type.
			deny: 	Enable the DoS prevention;
			allow: 	Disable the DoS prevention."
	DEFVAL  { allow } 
    ::= { dosEntry 2 }
       
			
	
	dnsGlobal         OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { sysDNS 1 }
	
   -- Rmon System

	dnsNameServerIPv4Addr OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      OCTET STRING
		MAX-ACCESS  read-write
		STATUS      current
		DESCRIPTION 
			  "The Object represents the Name server's IPv4 Address."
		   ::= { dnsGlobal 1 }

	dnsNameServerIPv6Addr OBJECT-TYPE
		SYNTAX      OCTET STRING
		MAX-ACCESS  read-write
		STATUS      current
		DESCRIPTION 
			  "The Object represents the Name server's IPv6 Address."
		   ::= { dnsGlobal 2 }		   
			
          

END
